# This page is for archive purposes, for initial images check [this page](initial-images-yocto.md)

# Pantavisor Initial Images(legacy)


Here, you can download our flashable base Pantavisor image for your device. For instructions on how to install one of these Pantavisor images, see our [how-to guide](choose-image.md).


Note that the images in these lists are generic and will later require the device to be [claimed](claim-device.md) if you want to interact with it from [Pantacor Hub](remote-control.md#pantacor-hub). If you prefer a customized image with a more streamlined remote setup, try our [download page](https://hub.pantacor.com/download-image).

## Stable Initial Images


This is our stable version images generated from the [initial devices](initial-devices.md).
